## ğŸ¤” What is Nano Banana Pro?

**Nano Banana Pro** is Google's latest multimodal AI model featuring:

- ğŸ¯ **Multimodal Understanding** - Process text, images, and video
- ğŸ¨ **High-Quality Generation** - Photorealistic to artistic styles
- âš¡ **Fast Iteration** - Quick edits and variations
- ğŸŒˆ **Diverse Styles** - From pixel art to oil paintings
- ğŸ”§ **Precise Control** - Detailed composition and lighting
- ğŸ“ **Complex Scenes** - Multi-object, multi-character rendering

ğŸ“š **Learn More:** [Nano Banana Pro: 10 Real Cases](https://youmind.com/blog/nano-banana-pro-10-real-cases)

### ğŸš€ Raycast Integration

Some prompts support **dynamic arguments** using [Raycast Snippets](https://raycast.com/help/snippets) syntax. Look for the ğŸš€ Raycast Friendly badge!

**Example:**
```
A quote card with "{argument name="quote" default="Stay hungry, stay foolish"}"
by {argument name="author" default="Steve Jobs"}
```

When used in Raycast, you can dynamically replace the arguments for quick iterations!

The portrait of the person is on the left, the text on the right. The text occupies two-thirds of the image and the portrait one-third, with a slight gradient transition effect on the portrait.

### No. 2: Premium liquid glass Bento grid product infographic with 8 modules

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

Create an Infographics with bento grid 8 module layout, user can specify any product name in Food, Medicine, tech etc category, choose language, Background style, Hero grid style

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Input Variable: [insert product name]
Language: [insert language]

System Instruction:
Create an image of premium liquid glass Bento grid product infographic with 8 modules (card 2 to 8 show text titles only).
1) Product Analysis:
â†’ Identify product's dominant natural color â†’ "hero color"
â†’ Identify category: FOOD / MEDICINE / TECH
2) Color Palette (derived from hero):
â†’ Product + accents: full saturation hero color
â†’ Icons, borders: muted hero (30-40% saturation, never black)
3) Visual Style:
â†’ Hero product: real photography (authentic, premium), 3D Glass version [choose one]
â†’ Cards: Apple liquid glass (85-90% transparent) with Whisper-thin borders and Subtle drop shadow for floating depth and reflecting the background color
â†’ Background stays behind cards and high blur where cards are [choose one]:
  - Ethereal: product essence, light caustics, abstract glow
  - Macro: product texture close-up, heavily blurred
  - Pattern: product repeated softly at 10-15% opacity
  - Context: relevant environment, blurred + desaturated
â†’ Add subtle motion effect
â†’ Asymmetric Bento grid, 16:9 landscape
â†’ Hero card: 28-30% | Info modules: 70-72%
4) Module Content (8 Cards):
M1 â€” Hero: Product displayed as real photo / 3D glass / stylized interpretation (choose one)in beautiful form + product name label
M2 â€” Core Benefits: 4 unique benefits + hero-color icons
M3 â€” How to Use: 4 usage methods + icons
M4 â€” Key Metrics: 5 EXACT data points
Format: [icon] [Label] [Bold Value] [Unit]
FOOD: Calories: [X] kcal/100g, Carbs: [X]g (fiber [X]g, sugar [X]g), Protein: [X]g, [Key Vitamin]: [X]mg ([X]% DV), [Key Mineral]: [X]mg ([X]% DV)
MEDICINE:Active: [name], Strength: [X] mg, Onset: [X] min, Duration: [X] hrs, Half-life: [X] hrs 
TECH:Chip: [model], Battery: [X] hrs, Weight: [X]g,[Key spec]: [value], Connectivity: [protocols]
M5 â€” Who It's For: 4 recommended groups with green checkmark icons | 3 caution groups with amber warning icons
M6 â€” Important Notes: 4 precautions + warning icons
M7 â€” Quick Reference:
â†’ FOOD: Glycemic Index + dietary tags with icons
â†’ MEDICINE: Side effects + severity with icons
â†’ TECH: Compatibility + certifications with icons
M8 â€” Did You Know: 3 facts (origin, science, global stat) + icons
Output: 1 image, 16:9 landscape, ultra-premium liquid glass infographic.
```

### No. 5: New Year's Day Special: Four-Panel Puzzle for 2026 Blessing

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed multi-panel prompt for Nano Banana Pro, creating a 2x2 grid photo collage where a single female character, in four different outfits and settings, pieces together a puzzle that spells '2026 New Year's Day Happy' in the center. The prompt specifies precise facial feature retention, clothing details, background elements, and photographic parameters for a fashion magazine style.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
[Key: Maintain precise facial features, retain original face structure, the character in the image must be completely consistent with the uploaded reference image] High-end photo studio 2x2 grid photo. Top-left panel (Navy Blue background): The character wears a navy blue uniform-style dress, decorated with gold buttons, vintage curls with a blue beret and pearl earrings. She holds up a huge puzzle piece (top-left piece, with the number "20" on it) with both hands, moving it towards the center of the frame. Her eyes are focused on the central puzzle area, her expression is serious, with a slight smile. The background features navy stripes, an anchor, and the text "Set Sail for the New Year". Top-right panel (Cherry Blossom Pink background): The same woman wears a pink lace dress, a pearl necklace, a princess hairstyle with a pink rose hairpin and crystal earrings. She holds up the top-right puzzle piece (with the number "26" on it) with both hands, moving it towards the center to connect with the top-left piece. Her eyes look at the puzzle seam, her expression is focused and expectant, and her body leans forward. The background features pink cherry blossoms, the text "Beautiful Encounter", butterflies, and petals. Bottom-left panel (Mint Green background): The same woman wears a mint green cotton and linen dress, in an artistic style, with natural long hair, a green hairband, and wooden earrings. She holds up the bottom-left puzzle piece (with the text "New Year's Day" on it) with both hands, moving it upwards to connect with the top-left piece. Her eyes look at the puzzle, her expression is serious, and her mouth is slightly pursed. The background features green plants, the text "Hope Grows", new sprouts, and leaves. Bottom-right panel (Lemon Yellow background): The same woman wears a yellow dress with a sunflower pattern, pigtails with yellow bows. She pushes in the last bottom-right puzzle piece (with the text "Happy" on it) to complete the puzzle. The four pieces perfectly form the complete pattern "2026 New Year's Day Happy" in the center of the frame. She tilts her head back, looking at the completed puzzle, her face beaming with a successful, joyful smile. The center of the frame bursts with golden light and confetti. The background features a yellow sun, the text "Complete Success", smiley faces, and sunflowers. The puzzle pieces converge from the four corners to the center to form a complete picture. Clear makeup, bright ring light, 85mm lens, f/1.8 aperture, four-panel composition with puzzle interaction, fashion magazine style.
```

### No. 6: Vintage Patent Document for an Invention

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

### No. 8: Detailed mirror-selfie otaku room scene

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A very detailed Nano Banana prompt describing a female mirror selfie in a blue-toned otaku computer corner, with full specifications for character, environment, lighting, camera, and negative prompts.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
### Scene
Mirror selfie in an otaku-style computer corner, blue color tone.

### Subject
* Gender expression: female
* Age: around 25
* Ethnicity: East Asian
* Body type: slim, with a defined waist; natural body proportions
* Skin tone: light neutral tone
* Hairstyle:
    * Length: waist-length hair
    * Style: straight with slightly curled ends
    * Color: medium brown
* Pose:
    * Stance: standing in a slight contrapposto pose
    * Right hand: holding a smartphone in front of her face (identity hidden)
    * Left arm: naturally hanging down alongside the torso
    * Torso: body leaning slightly back; waist and abdomen exposed
* Clothing:
    * Top: light blue cropped knit cardigan, top two buttons fastened; a blue French-style bra faintly visible
    * Bottom: denim ultra-short shorts, with a blue satin ribbon bow on each side of the hips
    * Socks: blue and white horizontal striped over-the-knee socks
    * Accessory: a blue cute mascot phone case

### Environment
* Description: bedroom computer corner seen through a wall-mounted mirror
* Furnishings:
    * White desk
    * Single monitor showing a soft blue wallpaper (no readable text)
    * Mechanical keyboard with white keycaps on a blue desk mat
    * Mouse on a small blue mouse pad
    * PC tower on the right side with blue case lighting
    * Three anime figures on or near the PC tower
    * A poster of a pagoda on the wall
    * Cat-shaped desk lamp with blue accents
    * A transparent glass of water
    * A tall green leafy plant by the window (on the left side of the frame)
* Color replacement: replace all originally pink elements (clothes and room decor) with blue tones (baby blue to sky blue/periwinkle blue).

### Lighting
* Light source: daylight coming from a large window on the left side of the camera, through sheer curtains
* Light quality: soft, diffused light
* White balance (K): 5200

### Camera
* Mode: smartphone rear camera shooting via the mirror (no portrait/bokeh mode)
* Equivalent focal length (mm): 26
* Distances (m):
    * Subject to mirror: 0.6
    * Camera to mirror: 0.5
* Exposure:
    * Aperture (f): 1.8
    * ISO: 100
    * Shutter speed (s): 0.01
    * Exposure compensation (EV): -0.3
* Focus: focus on the torso and shorts in the mirror image
* Depth of field: natural smartphone deep depth of field; background clearly visible with no artificial blur
* Composition:
    * Aspect ratio: 1:1
    * Crop: from the top of the head to mid-thigh; include the desk, monitor, PC tower, and plant in the frame
    * Angle: slightly high angle from the mirrorâ€™s point of view
    * Composition note: keep the subject centered; to avoid wide-angle edge distortion, have her stand a bit further away and crop to a square later.

### Negative prompts
* Any appearance of pink/magenta anywhere
* Beauty filters/over-smoothed skin; poreless skin look
* Exaggerated or distorted anatomy
* NSFW, see-through fabrics, wardrobe malfunctions
* Logos, brand names, or readable user interface text
* Fake portrait-mode blur, CGI/illustration feel
```

### No. 9: Edo-period Ukiyo-e reinterpretation of a modern scene

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly-structured image prompt to depict a modern-day scene reimagined as an Edo-period Japanese Ukiyo-e woodblock print, with detailed guidance on anachronistic tech, composition, texture, and color.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A Japanese Edo-period Ukiyo-e woodblock print. The overall feeling is a surreal collaboration between masters like Hokusai and Hiroshige, reimagining modern technology through an ancient lens.

**The scene:** {argument name="modern scene" default="a busy Shibuya scramble crossing"}

**Edo transformation logic:**
Characters wear Edo-era kimono but perform modern actions. All technology is transformed into surreal Edo equivalents:
* Smartphones are glowing, illustrated paper scrolls being read intently.
* Metro stations and trains are giant articulated wooden centipede carriages shuffling through crowds.
* Skyscrapers are reimagined as endless, towering wooden pagodas reaching into dramatic clouds.
* Robots and mecha appear as giant, armored woodblock golems.

The composition uses a flattened perspective with large, bold, hand-carved ink outlines. The background features heavily stylized Ukiyo-e wave patterns and dramatic, swirling clouds, with a distant Mt. Fuji visible on the horizon.

The image must look like a physical print, not a digital painting.
* Texture: strong visible wood grain texture and rough paper fibers throughout the piece.
* Printing imperfections: pigment bleeding is evident. Simulate hand-pressed plates with slight color misalignment for authenticity.
* Color palette: strictly limited to traditional mineral pigments, with dominant use of Prussian blue, vermilion red, and muted yellow ochre.
* Lighting: soft, flat, shadow-free lighting with no digital gradients.

Aspect ratio is 3:4 vertical poster. Include vertical Japanese calligraphy describing the scene and a traditional red artist seal stamp in a corner.
```

```
The subject's expression is calm and relaxed, with a natural, subtle smile. It looks as if she is about to start talking to the camera for a vlog. The image quality reflects a high-quality video shot indoors at night, with no filters, beautification effects, or artificial sharpening applied.
```

#### ğŸ“– Description

This prompt is designed to address a common issue in AI image generation where specifying 'iridescent' makes the entire subject glow. The goal is to generate an image of a butterfly (specifically a male *Atrophaneura alcinous* spring form) that accurately depicts selective structural color (iridescence) on the left wing and a matte brown color on the right wing, requiring precise control over light and texture.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Comparison of the front and back of a mounted specimen of a male {argument name="butterfly species" default="Atrophaneura alcinous"} spring form. The information in this illustration shows that the structural color on the left and the {argument name="color" default="matte brown"} on the right are the same butterfly. When you write 'iridescent' to the AI, everything shines. The job of the prompt is to specify 'this part shines, this part does not shine'.
```

### No. 53: YouTube Thumbnail - Seamless Cinematic Japanese Food Video Prompt

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A comprehensive, cinematic prompt used to generate a 4-cut video focused on Japanese cuisine, emphasizing ASMR elements, smooth transitions (match cuts/pans), warm lighting, and a minimalist piano soundtrack with Japanese instrument accents. The prompt was used for both image generation (Nano Banana Pro) and video generation (Kling 3.0 Omni).

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Generate a cinematic video focused on Japanese cuisine, consisting of four seamlessly connected cuts.

The first cut should be a close-up, carefully capturing cooking sounds, the rhythm of the knife, and the movement of hands touching the ingredients, starting with ASMR-like sound design that emphasizes steam and ingredient textures. The camera should use shallow depth of field and slow motion to naturally guide the viewer from the hands to the woman's gestures, showing her cuteness through small movements like subtle surprise or a gentle smile. Transition smoothly from here using match cuts or pans.

The second cut is a mid-shot of plating, beautifully capturing the movement of chopsticks and the moment ingredients are placed on the dish, emphasizing the delicate sounds of the dish and ingredients resonating, highlighting charm through carefulness and affection.

The subsequent cut uses an overhead composition to show the overall view of the finished dish, with the camera slowly zooming in, capturing the moment the woman takes a bite in a close-up, delicately capturing her breathing and subtle reactions to invite viewer empathy.

The final part connects to a warm interaction across the table, using a soft pan and crossfade to leave a lingering impression, subtly mixing laughter and fragments of conversation to express intimacy. The color tone should be filmic and warm-leaning, with natural lighting that keeps highlights gently suppressed. The music should be minimalist piano with Japanese instrument accents, and sound effects should carefully mix cooking and eating sounds to enhance realism. The overall tempo should be relaxed, prioritizing the natural connection of each cut's end to the next beginning through sound and movement.
```

### No. 73: Comic / Storyboard - Morning Routine Video Generation using Kling 3.0

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed video prompt generated by Freepik's assistant (GPT-5) based on an image from Nano Banana Pro, used to create a short film sequence with Kling 3.0. The prompt outlines three scenes focusing on smooth camera movements, close-ups of morning rituals, and a cinematic conclusion.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Scene 1
Use a smooth dolly shot to approach the window, transitioning from a long shot to a medium shot of the subject taking a deep breath in the morning light. Focus on subtle movements like relaxing the shoulders and finger reactions, creating an adorable atmosphere with distant natural sounds (birds chirping, wind) layered with delicate piano music. Crossfade to a close-up where the window light reflects on the fingertips.

Scene 2
Use close-ups focusing on steaming cups and small objects to rhythmically follow the hand movements (lifting the cup, stirring with a spoon, etc.). Use a combination of slow motion and light time-lapse to express warmth and innocence, layering sound effects like breathing and small laughs. The steam fills the screen and dissolves, leading to the next scene.

Scene 3
The camera pulls back to show the whole scene, concluding with the light movement of the subject ready to go out. Show the lingering atmosphere through the rhythm of steps and hand gestures, concluding cinematically with a backlit silhouette and soft color tones. The music gently fades out, leaving the lingering feeling of everyday life.
```

### No. 78: Comic / Storyboard - Detailed Cinematic Wuxia Scene Prompt: Dark Raven vs. Azure Frost

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

An extremely detailed, multi-scene prompt designed for cinematic video or image generation, focusing on a Wuxia (Chinese martial arts fantasy) style. It outlines five distinct camera shots, character actions, visual elements (heavy rain, ancient temple, lightning), camera movements (Dolly Shot, Crane Up, Bullet Time), dialogue, and sound effects for a dramatic confrontation between two characters, Dark Raven and Azure Frost.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Overall Style Prompt: Chinese Wuxia fantasy style, cinematic quality, motion blur, abandoned ancient temple in heavy rain, gloomy sky, lightning occasionally illuminating raindrops and broken eaves, the image is full of power and speed.

â€¢ Scene 1 (0-3 seconds): Dark Raven drags his sword, Azure Frost descends 
â€¢ Visuals: Rain pours down. Dark Raven wears heavy black armor emanating an ominous purple aura, dragging a massive chained dark iron greatsword with one hand. The blade scrapes the stone ground, creating dazzling sparks and ripples. His eyes are sinister as he looks ahead. Immediately after, Azure Frost lightly descends from the broken eaves of the ancient temple like a falling leaf. Her white and cyan tight-fitting outfit is sharp, her high ponytail flies, and the blue longsword in her hand is drawn with a 'zheng' sound, its cold aura pushing back the surrounding rain curtain. The two face off in the rain. 
â€¢ Cinematography: Extreme low-angle follow shot tracking the greatsword's path, then the camera quickly pulls back to show the full view of the confrontation in the rainy courtyardâ€”one black and heavy, the other cyan and light. 
â€¢ Dialogue/Sound Effects: Dark Raven (low and hoarse): "{argument name="Dark Raven dialogue" default="You are beyond redemption."}" 
â€¢ Sound Effects: Heavy metal scraping, torrential rain, wind. 

â€¢ Scene 2 (3-6 seconds): Greatsword sweeps, light sword strikes like a flash â€¢ Visuals: Dark Raven suddenly exerts force, swinging the greatsword with both arms. A crescent-shaped black sword energy tears through the rain curtain and sweeps out. Raindrops evaporate in its path, and the stone ground is plowed open. Azure Frost's eyes narrow. Tapping the water surface with her toe, her body shoots up like a kite, executing a nimble side flip in the air, narrowly avoiding the sword energy. At the same time, using the momentum of her descent, the cold light of her sword tip condenses, striking straight at Dark Raven's throat like a meteor. 
â€¢ Cinematography: Fast-paced cuts. First, a side follow shot (Dolly Shot) captures the black sword energy slicing countless raindrops in slow motion, then switches to a high-angle view, showing the graceful trajectory of Azure Frost's aerial evasion and counterattack.
â€¢ Sound Effects: Heavy whistling of the greatsword cutting the air, 'chichi' sound of sword energy evaporating, sound of clothes tearing the wind. 

â€¢ Scene 3 (6-9 seconds): Mid-air clash, sparks fly â€¢ Visuals: Dark Raven swings his greatsword back, colliding precisely with Azure Frost's descending longsword! "Clangâ€”!" The immense power of the greatsword fiercely clashes with the nimble cold aura of the longsword, erupting in dazzling blue-white sparks and a shockwave that pushes away all the surrounding rain. Dark Raven presses down with his strength advantage, while Azure Frost uses her light footwork, tapping the greatsword with her toe, using the force to backflip and resolve the immense pressure. 
â€¢ Cinematography: Orbiting shot (Bullet Time). The camera centers on the point of weapon collision, rotating 360 degrees rapidly, finally freezing on a close-up of the moment of maximum sparks and the two forces counteracting. 
â€¢ Dialogue/Sound Effects: Azure Frost (cold and firm): "{argument name="Azure Frost dialogue" default="Evil will not prevail!"}" 
â€¢ Sound Effects: Huge metal collision roar, humming sound of power confrontation. 

â€¢ Scene 4 (9-12 seconds): Azure shadows continuous, black wall defends â€¢ Visuals: The moment she lands, Azure Frost launches an attack. Her figure turns into a cyan afterimage, her longsword stabs rapidly, instantly transforming into several fierce cyan sword lights attacking Dark Raven from different angles. The cold aura of the sword tips leaves streaks of frost in the air. Dark Raven lets out a low roar, swinging the heavy greatsword into an impenetrable barrier, forming a purple-black sword energy shield. Amidst the dense 'ding-dang' sounds, the cyan sword lights are all blocked, but the powerful impact still forces Dark Raven to retreat three steps, each step crushing the stone bricks beneath his feet. 
â€¢ Cinematography: One-shot handheld follow shot (Shaky Cam). The camera closely follows Azure Frost's attack trajectory, with slight shaking accompanying each stab, then quickly pans to Dark Raven's defense and retreat, creating a strong sense of immersion. 
â€¢ Sound Effects: Dense, crisp sound of sword tips hitting the barrier, sound of stone bricks cracking, heavy footsteps and panting. 

â€¢ Scene 5 (12-15 seconds): Ultimate collision, swallowing the universe â€¢ Visuals: Dark Raven is enraged, injecting all his purple energy into the greatsword, plunging it into the ground! Boom! A thick purple-black light column shoots up into the sky, stirring the clouds above. Azure Frost shows no fear, pouring all her cold energy into her sword. Man and sword become one, transforming into a massive, pure cyan stream of light, descending like a comet, striking straight at the center of the light column. The two collide with a roar! Time seems to stand still, followed by an explosive, blinding white light and a circular airwave that sweeps away all the rain, debris, and dead leaves in the entire courtyard. 
â€¢ Cinematography: Rapid close-up zoom out. First, quick cuts between close-ups of Dark Raven's cold eyes and Azure Frost's determined eyes, then the camera rapidly pulls up and back like a rocket (Crane Up), turning into a distant overhead view, showing the shocking full scene of the expanding white light and the airwave sweeping across the ruins of the ancient temple. The image freezes at the peak of the white light. 
â€¢ Dialogue/Sound Effects: (Before collision) Dark Raven's roar and Azure Frost's clear shout intertwine.
â€¢ Sound Effects: Humming sound of energy convergence, earth-shattering explosion, followed by all sounds fading, leaving only the receding echo of the rain.
```

```
â‘  Create a "{argument name="character 1" default="Polar Bear"}" and a "{argument name="character 2" default="Panda"}" wearing ice skates, and the background location. Normal chat-based input is also OK. Whether you generate it all at once or separately, the process is the same.

â‘¡ Perform annotation on the image.
This is the most troublesome part, so I made it a tool.
Based on the file name, I create a prompt that organizes "which part of which image to reference."
(Pose / BG / Face / Clothing, etc.)

â‘¢ Add supplementary information such as composition and color scheme for the final generation.
```

### No. 81: Comic / Storyboard - Comic Book Poster Illustration Template

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A structured JSON prompt template for Nano Banana Pro, designed to generate a dynamic, modern comic book poster illustration (16:9 aspect ratio) with a collage of comic panels, halftone effects, and dramatic lighting. It includes placeholders for the main character, title, and specific panel content, and requires strict identity preservation from a reference image.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "meta": {
    "purpose": "Comic book poster illustration for viral sci-fi storytelling or graphic novels",
    "style": "Modern comic/graphic novel with halftone and dynamic effects, 4K resolution"
  },
  "reference_image": {
    "use": true,
    "identity_preservation": "strict",
    "face_similarity": "high"
  },
  "canvas": {
    "aspect_ratio": "16:9",
    "orientation": "horizontal poster"
  },
  "title_text": {
    "text": "{argument name="title text" default="ZOOM!!! OR Your Title"}",
    "position": "top_center",
    "style": "bold comic lettering, thick hand-drawn font",
    "color": "cream white with black outline",
    "effects": ["3D emboss", "ink shadow", "halftone texture"]
  },
  "main_character": {
    "subject": "{argument name="main character" default="Space pilot with metallic implant OR Your hero"}",
    "pose": "[e.g., Angry heroic OR Dynamic action]",
    "lighting": "dramatic rim lighting",
    "render_style": "Japanese Anime comic illustration"
  },
  "comic_panels": [
    {
      "position": "top_left",
      "subject": "[e.g., Extreme close-up behind cracked glass]",
      "expression": "[e.g., Angry]",
      "panel_effect": "[e.g., Burst explosion, sound effect CRAAACK]"
    },
    {
      "position": "top_right",
      "subject": "[e.g., Pilot mouth open]",
      "expression": "[e.g., Worried]",
      "speech_text": "[e.g., NOOO!]"
    },
    {
      "position": "bottom_left",
      "subject": "[e.g., Spacecraft profile]",
      "speech_text": "[e.g., WHAAA?!]",
      "motion_lines": true
    },
    {
      "position": "bottom_right",
      "subject": "[e.g., Pilot scared]",
      "speech_text": "[e.g., LAZARUS!]",
      "panel_effect": "[e.g., Starburst]"
    }
  ],
  "background": {
    "style": "comic panels collage",
    "colors": ["orange", "yellow", "blue", "teal"],
    "elements": ["halftone dots", "ink splashes", "action lines", "explosion shapes"],
    "bottom_scene": "[e.g., Asteroid field with gold veins]"
  },
  "art_style": {
    "genre": "modern comic book",
    "influences": ["Marvel covers", "DC posters", "Pop-art"],
    "line_work": "clean bold outlines",
    "shading": "soft painterly with halftone"
  },
  "render_quality": {
    "detail_level": "high",
    "sharpness": "crisp",
    "color_grading": "vibrant cinematic"
  },
  "constraints": {
    "no_blur": true,
    "no_extra_faces": true,
    "no_watermark": true
  },
  "negative_prompt": ["low quality", "blurry", "extra limbs", "distorted face", "bad anatomy", "realistic photo"]
}
```

### No. 84: Product Marketing - High-Fashion Editorial Shot on City Sidewalk Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A complex, multi-part prompt for Nano Banana Pro designed to generate a high-fashion editorial image. It requires a reference photo for the main character's identity and specifies detailed elements including pose (squatting low), outfit (low-back thong bodysuit), urban environment, and cinematography (golden hour backlight, high contrast).

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "image": {
    "main_description": "A high-fashion editorial shot of a woman in a provocative pose on a modern city sidewalk at dusk, featuring dramatic backlighting and a sleek, minimalist aesthetic.",
    "characters": {
      "main_reference_character": {
        "identity_anchor": "The character based on the provided reference photo, preserving strictly the user's identity source.",
        "ethnicity_and_phenotype": "Determined by the user provided reference photo.",
        "face_and_skin": "Skin texture and lighting interaction consistent with the scene, but facial features are strictly derived from the reference.",
        "expression": "A confident, over-the-shoulder sultry gaze toward the camera through black-rimmed rectangular glasses.",
        "hair": "Voluminous, long layered hair with soft waves and significant body, styled in a glamorous blowout.",
        "body_and_pose": "Squatting low to the ground on the balls of the feet, torso twisted back toward the camera to showcase the back, one hand resting lightly on the knee.",
        "outfit": "A white, ultra-low-back thong bodysuit with thin spaghetti straps, paired with low-rise black tailored trousers and black strappy high-heel sandals with metallic stiletto heels."
      },
      "supporting_characters": []
    },
    "text_elements": {
      "content": "{argument name="text content" default="76"}",
      "typography": "Thin, minimalist sans-serif font.",
      "placement": "Etched or mounted on the grey marble pillar in the background.",
      "integration": "Subtle architectural detail, blending naturally with the building exterior."
    },
    "environment": {
      "location": "Upscale urban sidewalk adjacent to a modern building with marble and glass facades.",
      "elements": "Concrete pavement slabs, a large potted shrub, distant palm trees lining a street, parked cars in the far background.",
      "atmosphere": "Clear, twilight air with the soft glow of a setting sun in the distance."
    },
    "cinematography": {
      "lighting_setup": "Warm golden hour backlight creating a rim light effect on the hair; soft, cool fill light on the subject's face and back.",
      "color_grading": "Muted urban tones with high contrast; deep blacks and bright whites against a neutral concrete and marble palette.",
      "shadows_and_highlights": "Soft shadows stretching across the pavement; sharp specular highlights on the metallic heels and glasses frames.",
      "reflections": "Subtle reflections on the glass windows and polished marble surfaces."
    },
    "camera_and_tech": {
      "framing": "Full shot, wide-angle lens, low camera height looking slightly upward at the subject.",
      "optics": "35mm focal length, f/2.8 for a moderate depth of field that keeps the background recognizable but soft.",
      "visual_fidelity": "8k resolution, raw photo, realistic skin pores, sharp focus on the subject, slight film grain."
    },
    "style_and_mood": {
      "aesthetic": "High-end fash"
    }
  }
}
```

### No. 93: E-commerce Main Image - Macro Hero Shot of Optical Cast Glass Object with Caustics

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly technical prompt for generating an ultra-close macro hero shot of a specified subject rendered as premium optical cast glass, focusing on controlled internal highlights, strong rainbow caustics cast onto the surface, and preserving crisp edge details without distortion.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Task: Ultra-close macro hero shot of a {argument name="subject" default="SUBJECT"} as premium optical cast glass with diagonal light-band shadows, stronger rainbow caustics, and clean readable high-detail areas (no refraction â€œmushâ€). Subject is FULLY visible and NOT cropped. The subject is placed on the surface or floating in the air at a low altitude above the surface.
Style: Photoreal luxury product; seamless blue-gray gradient background #9FAFBC (cool, slightly blue, low saturation); glossy reflective plane; smooth clear optical glass with crisp edges, controlled internal highlights, subtle star glints; pronounced caustic streaks + vivid prismatic rainbow arcs cast onto the surface from the subject.
Framing: extreme close-up, subject fills ~90â€“95% of the frame, fully visible and not cropped.
Readability (fix mush): preserve crisp facial/edge detailsâ€”minimize internal warping, lensing, and overlapping caustic patterns on fine features; keep the interior visually â€œquietâ€ so the surface sculpt reads clean.
Optical control: low-distortion, low-aberration glass look (reduced dispersion inside the object) with strong external caustics on the surface.
Lighting: broad diagonal soft light bands; long soft cast shadow with smooth penumbra; rainbow caustics should be stronger and more numerous around the base and across the floor. Clean white color.
Environment control: seamless studio only; gray/black flags controlling reflections; no window/room elements.
Negative prompt: excessive refraction, heavy distortion, lens effect, warped facial features, chaotic highlights, milky/foggy glass, random reflections, window, interior, wall corner, faceted, polygonal, low poly, text, watermark, clutter
```

### No. 102: E-commerce Main Image - Chrome Ripple Flow Product Photography Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A complex product photography prompt focusing on generating a floating product with matte black and metallic silver finishes, centrally placed within a single, continuous, undulating background surface featuring a fine ribbed texture and a seamless duotone color gradient.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "image_generation_request": {
    "subject": "{argument name="product name" default="PRODUCT"}",
    "product_finish": {
      "primary": "matte black with subtle light absorption",
      "secondary": "polished metallic silver with mirror-like reflections",
      "treatment": "duotone â€” matte black body with metallic silver accents, trim, edges, or panel insets"
    },
    "composition": {
      "placement": "dead center, full view, floating suspended within the folded surface environment",
      "scale": "product occupies roughly 30-40% of the frame",
      "constraints": [
        "product must be entirely visible with no cropping",
        "no pedestals, stands, platforms, or ground planes",
        "the surface folds frame the product but never obscure more than 10% of it",
        "product is the sharpest element in the scene"
      ]
    },
    "background_environment": {
      "description": "A single continuous undulating surface that fills the entire frame, folding over and around itself in large voluminous waves â€” like a massive sheet of pleated metallic silk or a single machined metal panel that has been softly twisted and draped. This is NOT multiple separate ribbons or strands. It is ONE connected surface.",
      "base_color": "{argument name="deep background color" default="INSERT DEEP BACKGROUND COLOR visible in crevices â€” e.g. pure black, midnight navy"}",
      "surface_color_1": "{argument name="gradient color A" default="INSERT GRADIENT COLOR A â€” e.g. soft lavender, warm copper, pearl rose"}",
      "surface_color_2": "[INSERT GRADIENT COLOR B â€” e.g. deep indigo, cobalt blue, violet]",
      "color_behavior": "The two colors blend in a smooth continuous gradient across the single surface, shifting based on the surface's curvature and light angle. Where the surface faces the light it shows color_1, where it curves away it transitions to color_2. The transition is seamless with no hard edges or stripes.",
      "surface_texture": {
        "type": "fine parallel ribs embossed into the surface â€” like the grooves on a vinyl record or finely pleated accordion fabric",
        "rib_description": "extremely fine, uniform, tightly spaced parallel lines that follow the flow direction of the surface. The ribs are a TEXTURE on the surface, not separate objects. They create a subtle corrugated micro-relief that catches light along each tiny ridge.",
        "rib_density": "very high â€” approximately 50-100 visible lines per inch of surface, creating a dense linear grain",
        "rib_depth": "shallow â€” the ribs are subtle surface detail, not deep cuts. They create gentle highlight-shadow alternation across the surface"
      },
```

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly explicit JSON prompt for generating a photorealistic portrait of a woman (Megan Fox resemblance) in a Batgirl-inspired bodysuit with exaggerated hourglass proportions (large bust, wide hips). It specifies the costume details (black/purple/yellow, halter-neck), pose (weight shifted, hand on granite countertop), and environment (indoor bathroom with comic poster), using negative prompts to ensure unstyled, physical proportions.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "subject": {
    "desc": "Megan Fox resemblance, fair skin, long straight dark brown/black hair over shoulders/back, symmetrical face with full lips, defined brows, green-hazel eyes, tiny Batgirl mask covering eyes",
    "apparel": {
      "item": "Batgirl inspired bodysuit",
      "style": "Halter-neck sleeveless, high-cut legs",

    },

      "skin": "Smooth fair with natural tone variation"
    }
  },

    "posture": "Standing upright, weight shifted to right hip (viewer's left) for pelvic tilt, torso slightly angled toward camera",

      "right_arm": "Extended down, hand resting on granite countertop",
      "left_arm": "Hanging naturally by side, partially obscured by hip",
      "head": "Slight tilt, facing forward"
    },

  },
  "environment": {
    "location": "Indoor bathroom",
    "elements": [

      "Wooden door with tall frosted glass panel (right background)",
      "Towel bar (background left)",
      "Large Wonder Woman comic poster on black walls, small neon 'KeorUnreal' sign"
    ]
  },
  "camera": {
    "shot": "Medium (thighs up), vertical 3:4",
    "angle": "Eye-level slightly frontal",
    "lens": "50-85mm portrait",
    "dof": "Moderate, sharp subject, slightly soft distinct background",
    "framing": "Centered subject"

  "lighting": "Soft diffuse indoor artificial, overhead/slightly frontal, even illumination, soft shadows under bust/hips, highlights on body contours and fabric sheen",
  "mood": "Confident calm sultry, casual intimate domestic atmosphere",
  "style": "Photorealistic smartphone photography, high-fidelity detailed fabric/skin textures, natural color grading, unstyled physical proportions",
  "colors": "Black suit with vibrant yellow/purple accents dominant, green/black granite, warm wood, neutral walls, natural contrast/saturation",
  "quality": "High-def sharp focus on eyes/face/suit pattern, low noise, minimal grain",
  "negative_prompt": "small/reduced/flattened bust, lifted breasts, slimmed torso/hips, proportion averaging, plastic/airbrushed skin, beautification, stylization, depth flattening, wide distortion, mirror selfies, phone-in-hand, reflections"
```

### No. 119: Game Asset - Pixar-Style Giant World Character Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A prompt for generating a Pixar-style 3D animation or Claymation image of a character holding an object as a helmet in a giant-sized world. It specifies golden hour lighting, vibrant acid pop colors, and technical camera details like a telephoto lens for background compression.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
## SUBJECT & ACTION
{argument name="character" default="[CHARACTER]"} holding a {argument name="object" default="[OBJECT]"} as a helmet and looking very ready for battle.
The character looks determined but confused.

## ENVIRONMENT & CONTEXT
Scene takes place in a world where everything is giant sized.
Background details: overgrown vegetation, blurred crowd.

## VISUAL STYLE & AESTHETIC
**Style:** Pixar-Style 3D Animation or Claymation
**Lighting:** Golden Hour with God Rays breaking through dust particles
**Camera:** Telephoto 200mm (Compressed background, subject isolation, bokeh)
**Color Palette:** Vibrant Acid Pop Colors (Pink, Lime, Yellow)

## DETAILS & TEXTURE
- Focus on textures: Gritty concrete and rusting metal with peeling paint
- Fluffy fur texture
- High fidelity, 8k, extremely detailed masterpiece.

## PARAMETERS
--ar 3:2 --chaos 20 --style raw
```

#### ğŸ–¼ï¸ Generated Images

##### Image 1

<div align="center">
<img src="https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771050462016_e9dt71_HBCx2-JXwAE0oTq.jpg" width="600" alt="Game Asset - Pixar-Style Giant World Character Prompt - Image 1">
</div>

#### ğŸ“Œ Details

- **Author:** [Dominus the Prompter](https://x.com/iamdomprompt)
- **Source:** [Twitter Post](https://x.com/iamdomprompt/status/2022311833479066017)

### No. 120: Game Asset - 3D Anthropomorphic Dog in Streetwear

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A prompt for generating a full-body 3D stylized anthropomorphic cartoon dog character wearing modern streetwear, focusing on high detail, Pixar-quality rendering, and a clean, fashion editorial aesthetic.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Full-body 3D stylized anthropomorphic cartoon dog character wearing modern streetwear, oversized neon green hoodie, cargo pants, chunky sneakers, reflective sunglasses, silver chain necklace. Confident relaxed pose with hands in pockets. Minimal studio background in solid lime green. Soft studio lighting, smooth shadows, high detail fabric texture, Pixar-quality 3D render, ultra-clean composition, centered framing, fashion editorial character design, 8K resolution.
```

## ğŸ¤ How to Contribute

We welcome contributions! You can submit prompts via:

### ğŸ› GitHub Issue

1. Click [**Submit New Prompt**](https://github.com/YouMind-OpenLab/awesome-nano-banana-pro-prompts/issues/new?template=submit-prompt.yml)
2. Fill in the form with prompt details and image
3. Submit and wait for team review
4. If approved (we'll add `approved` label), it will automatically sync to CMS
5. Your prompt will appear in README within 4 hours

**Note:** We only accept submissions via GitHub Issues to ensure quality control.

See [CONTRIBUTING.md](docs/CONTRIBUTING.md) for detailed guidelines.
